       <div id="tab-events">
        <div class="tabHeader eventsHeader">

        <div class="tabContent">
         <h2>
          Upcoming Webinars
         </h2>
         <div>
         </div>
         <div>
          <p>
           <strong>
            <img alt="" class="alignright wp-image-32188 size-thumbnail" height="150" src="http://wolf.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/jun2118-150x150.jpg" width="150"/>
            <a href="https://events.r20.constantcontact.com/register/eventReg?oeidk=a07eergcea960f8f8c9&amp;oseq=&amp;c=&amp;ch=">
             Summer Solstice Webinar
            </a>
            <br/>
           </strong>
           Thursday, June 21, 2018 – 6 p.m. CDT
           <strong>
            <br/>
            Webinar rate:
           </strong>
           $15 Non-members, $12 Members
           <strong>
            <br/>
           </strong>
          </p>
          <p>
           The summer solstice is the longest day of the year in the northern hemisphere and marks the start of the summer. For wolves, this is a challenging time of year. Wolves have evolved to have hair throughout their body with no sweat glands to aid in cooling. Wolves rely on panting to evaporate heat from their tongue and spend the warmest parts of the day resting in some cool sand. Join us for this one-hour webinar as we employ some techniques to keep the pack cool.
          </p>
         </div>
         <hr/>
         <h2>
          Upcoming Wolf Conference
         </h2>
         <p>
          <strong>
           <a href="http://www.wolf.org/programs/symposium-2018/">
            International Wolf Symposium
           </a>
          </strong>
          <br/>
          October 11-14, 2018
         </p>
         <hr/>
         <h2>
         </h2>
         <h2>
          Upcoming Adventure Programs
         </h2>
         <p class="pageName">
         </p>
         <p>
          <img alt="" class="size-thumbnail wp-image-13385 alignright" height="150" src="http://wolf.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/Daniele_Wolf_WildKids-150x150.jpg" width="150"/>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           <a href="http://www.wolf.org/programs/learning-adventures/jr-biologist-day-camp/">
            Jr. Biologist Summer Camp
           </a>
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Date:
          </strong>
          July 16 – 19, 2018
          <strong>
           <br/>
          </strong>
          <strong>
           Time:
          </strong>
          Monday – Thursday,
          <strong>
          </strong>
          8:15 a.m. CDT– 3:30 p.m. CDT
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Registration Deadline:
          </strong>
          July 2, 2018
          <br/>
          <b>
           Program Rates:
          </b>
          Non-member $150, Member $140
         </p>
         <p>
          Time to unplug your kids from the virtual world and reconnect them with the real one by joining us at our four day Jr. Wolf Biologist Summer Camp! Participants will learn about wolves and other animals through hands-on outdoor activities during this summer program.
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.wolf.org/programs/learning-adventures/wildlife-career-day/">
           <strong>
            <img alt="" class="alignright size-thumbnail wp-image-19629" height="150" src="http://wolf.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/shannon-150x150.jpg" width="150"/>
            Wildlife Career Day
           </strong>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Date:
          </strong>
          August 4, 2018
          <strong>
           <br/>
          </strong>
          <strong>
           Time:
          </strong>
          Saturday, 8:00 a.m. – 8:00 p.m. CDT
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Registration Deadline:
          </strong>
          July 21, 2018
         </p>
         <p>
          <b>
           Program Rates:
          </b>
          Non-member $40, Member $35
         </p>
         <p>
          Are you interested in science, biology or working with wildlife? Join our Wildlife Career Day and meet local biologists, conservation officers, veterinarians and animal caretakers. You’ll get a special behind the scenes tour to learn more about our wolves and even create an enrichment activity for our wolves to try! Wrap-up your day by watching our wolves be fed their weekly meal at What’s for Dinner?
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           <a href="http://www.wolf.org/programs/learning-adventures/women_wolves_bwa/">
            <img alt="" class="alignright wp-image-29031 size-thumbnail" height="150" src="http://wolf.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/01/Tim-DonovanFWC_women_canoe-150x150.jpg" width="150"/>
           </a>
           <a href="http://www.wolf.org/programs/learning-adventures/women_wolves_bwa/">
            Wolves and Women’s Weekend: Boundary Waters Adventure
           </a>
           <br/>
          </strong>
          <strong>
           Date:
          </strong>
          September 14-16, 2018
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Time:
          </strong>
          Friday 4 p.m. CDT– Sunday 9:00 a.m. CDT
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Registration Deadline:
          </strong>
          September 1, 2018
          <br/>
          <b>
           Program Rates:
          </b>
          Non-member $250, Member $225
         </p>
         <p>
          Join us for a fun, relaxing weekend learning about wolves and the northwoods while enjoying the company of women who have the same hectic routine as you! Slow it down for the weekend, enjoy some wine and cheese as we gather at the Northern Tier High Adventure Canoe Base. Participate in a weekend full of canoeing, radio telemetry, and trekking through the beautiful northwoods! Enjoy everything the wilderness has to offer on this outdoor adventure!
         </p>
         <p>
          <span style="border-radius: 2px; text-indent: 20px; width: auto; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: center; font: bold 11px/20px 'Helvetica Neue',Helvetica,sans-serif; color: #ffffff; background: #bd081c  no-repeat scroll 3px 50% / 14px 14px; position: absolute; opacity: 1; z-index: 8675309; display: none; cursor: pointer;">

         <h2>
          Gift Memberships…Kindness They’ll Remember All Year Long
         </h2>
         <p>
          International Wolf Center members drive the effort to teach the science-based facts about wolves. A membership to the International Wolf Center makes a perfect gift for any wolf enthusiast.
         </p>
         <p>
          For an entire year, your gift recipient will enjoy:
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           A one-year subscription to
           <a href="http://www.wolf.org/wolf-info/wolf-magazine/">
            I
            <em>
             nternational Wolf
            </em>
           </a>
           magazine
          </li>
          <li>
           Free admission to the International Wolf Center in Ely, MN
          </li>
          <li>
           Discounts on
           <a href="http://www.wolf.org/programs/learning-adventures/">
            Adventure Programs
           </a>
           and
           <a href="http://shop.wolf.org">
            Wolf Den Store
           </a>
           purchases
          </li>
